# selfhost.directory

**A curated, searchable directory of self-hostable projects — run open-source apps on your own server.**

---

[**selfhost.directory**](https://selfhost.directory) catalogues thousands of **open-source, self-hostable projects** across many categories — each with setup guides, alternatives, licences, host platforms and live version and update tracking. If you want to ditch a SaaS subscription and run it yourself, start here.

## 💡 Why selfhost.directory? 💡

- **Curated, not a dump** — real descriptions, setup difficulty, host platform and licence for every app.
- **Live version and update tracking** — see the latest release and how actively a project is maintained.
- **Find alternatives** — every app links to self-hostable alternatives so you can compare before you deploy.

<div align="center">

### Find your next self-hosted app

**[selfhost.directory →](https://selfhost.directory)**

<sub>Run open-source software on your own server. Own your data!</sub>

</div>
